<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200"></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/banana" class="extiw" title="w:banana">banana</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/banana" class="extiw" title="w:banana">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wolof_language" class="extiw" title="w:Wolof language">Wolof</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="wo"><a href="/wiki/banaana#Wolof" title="banaana">banaana</a></i>, via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Bananavarieties.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Bananavarieties.jpg/220px-Bananavarieties.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="126" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/de/Bananavarieties.jpg/330px-Bananavarieties.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/d/de/Bananavarieties.jpg 2x" data-file-width="387" data-file-height="221"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Bananavarieties.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Four different types of bananas. The larger yellow bananas on the far right are commercially dominant Cavendish bananas.</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Received_Pronunciation" class="extiw" title="w:Received Pronunciation">Received Pronunciation</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">bə-näʹnə</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/bəˈnɑːnə/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General_American" class="extiw" title="w:General American">General American</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">bə-năʹnə</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/bəˈnænə/</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">banana</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a> and <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/bananas#English" title="bananas">bananas</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An elongated curved <a href="/wiki/tropical" title="tropical">tropical</a> <a href="/wiki/fruit" title="fruit">fruit</a> of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Musa" class="extiw" title="w:Musa">banana plant</a> that grows in bunches and has a creamy flesh and a smooth skin.
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>, <a href="/wiki/American_English" title="American English">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ireland" class="extiw" title="w:Ireland">Ireland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Especially, the sweet, yellow fruit of the Cavendish banana <a href="/wiki/cultivar" title="cultivar">cultivar</a>.</li></ol></li>
<li>The tropical tree-like plant which bears clusters of bananas. The plant, usually of the genus <i><a href="/wiki/Musa" title="Musa">Musa</a></i> but sometimes also including plants from <i><a href="/wiki/Ensete" title="Ensete">Ensete</a></i>, has large, elongated leaves and is related to the <a href="/wiki/plantain" title="plantain">plantain</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A yellow colour, like that of a banana's skin.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel">banana: <span style="background-color:#FFE135; display:inline-block; width:80px;">&nbsp;</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mildly <a href="/wiki/derogatory" title="derogatory">derogatory</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/ethnic" title="ethnic">ethnic</a> <a href="/wiki/slur" title="slur">slur</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A person of Asian descent, especially a <a href="/wiki/Chinese" title="Chinese">Chinese</a> <a href="/wiki/American" title="American">American</a>, who has assimilated into Western culture or married a <a href="/wiki/Caucasian" title="Caucasian">Caucasian</a> (from the "yellow" outside and "white" inside). Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/coconut#English" title="coconut">coconut</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">assimilated Hispanic or Black</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/Oreo#English" title="Oreo">Oreo</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Black person who is "black outside" and "white inside"</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/nuclear_physics" title="nuclear physics">nuclear physics</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/banana_equivalent_dose" title="banana equivalent dose">banana equivalent dose</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#colloquial" title="Appendix:Glossary">colloquial</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/catamorphism" title="catamorphism">catamorphism</a> (from the use of <a href="/wiki/banana_bracket" title="banana bracket">banana brackets</a> in the notation).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a href="/wiki/penis" title="penis">penis</a>.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1986</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=_6cgAQAAMAAJ">Cop Feels of Three Men's "Privates"</a> Christopher Street - Volume 10
<dl><dd>The fact that the cop bought O'Brien a beer after feeling of his <b>banana</b> suggests that it must have been a promising one</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2012</b> Sarah Miynowski <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=lg0mATRb6EAC&amp;pg=PT36">Fishbowl</a> page 36
<dl><dd>His you-know-what turned soft .. his eight o'clock class was the last thing on his mind five minutes ago, when his <b>banana</b> wasn't overripe.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2014</b> Anthony Bunko <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=MdBxBAAAQBAJ&amp;pg=PT71">Lord Forgive Me</a> page 71
<dl><dd>Most of the gang were trying their best to shag the girls. One boy was sitting in a tree playing with himself and another was asking a table of teenagers if they would like to see his <b>banana</b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2017</b> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=4pQ4DwAAQBAJ&amp;pg=PA234">Intimate Relationships in Cinema, Literature and Visual Culture</a> page 234
<dl><dd>He adds that after eating his <b>banana</b> (sucking his penis), he wants anal sex, but she asks him to lick her pussy. Then he tells her no because it is disgusting.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/sports" title="sports">sports</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href="/wiki/banana_kick" title="banana kick">banana kick</a>.</li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Adjective">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">banana</strong> (<i>not <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#comparable" title="Appendix:Glossary">comparable</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Curved like a banana, especially of a ball in flight.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>2001</b>, Rayne Barton, <i>The Green Hills Golf Chronicles</i>, page 155, <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0738847917" title="Special:BookSources/0738847917">→ISBN</a>.
<dl><dd>Even the lowly <b>banana</b> ball, the bane of so many weekenders, sometimes can be exactly right, as in this case.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2002</b>, Andrew Collins, <i>Guild of Honor</i>, page 53, <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/1403371490" title="Special:BookSources/1403371490">→ISBN</a>.
<dl><dd>He played the fading, low-<b>banana</b> shot as planned, and the ball whistled left of the oak tree and between the pines.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2006</b>, Richard Witzig, <i>The Global Art of Soccer</i>, page 247, <a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0977668800" title="Special:BookSources/0977668800">→ISBN</a>.
<dl><dd>[...]Bernd Schneider closed the scoring in injury-time with a 23 meter free-kick <b>banana</b> shot into the upper-right corner.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Lower_Sorbian">Lower Sorbian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Lower Sorbian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href="/wiki/Banane#German" title="Banane">Banane</a></i>, from ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wolof_language" class="extiw" title="w:Wolof language">Wolof</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="wo"><a href="/wiki/banaana#Wolof" title="banaana">banaana</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_7">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Lower_Sorbian_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Lower Sorbian pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/baˈnana/</span></li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Portuguese">Portuguese</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Portuguese">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Banana.arp.750pix.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Banana.arp.750pix.jpg/220px-Banana.arp.750pix.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="157" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Banana.arp.750pix.jpg/330px-Banana.arp.750pix.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Banana.arp.750pix.jpg/440px-Banana.arp.750pix.jpg 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="536"></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Banana.arp.750pix.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>bananas</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Uncertain. Possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wolof_language" class="extiw" title="w:Wolof language">Wolof</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="wo"><a href="/wiki/banaana#Wolof" title="banaana">banaana</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">banana</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar"><a href="/wiki/%D8%A8%D9%86%D8%A7%D9%86#Arabic" title="بنان">بَنَان</a></i>‎ <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">banān</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fingertip, banana</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_9">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/European_Portuguese" class="extiw" title="w:European Portuguese">Portugal</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Portuguese_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Portuguese pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/bɐˈnɐ.nɐ/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brazilian_Portuguese" class="extiw" title="w:Brazilian Portuguese">Brazil</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Portuguese_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Portuguese pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/baˈnɐ.nɐ/</span>, <span class="IPA">/bɐˈnɐ.nɐ/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_12">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="pt">banana</strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-pt p-form-of" lang="pt"><a href="/wiki/bananas#Portuguese" title="bananas">bananas</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="#English">banana</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">fruit</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="pt"><b>Bananas</b> são ricas em potássio</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Bananas</b> are high in potassium</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href="#English">banana</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">plant</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="pt"><a href="/wiki/bananeira#Portuguese" title="bananeira">bananeira</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">more common</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#informal" title="Appendix:Glossary">informal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/penis" title="penis">penis</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brazil" class="extiw" title="w:Brazil">Brazil</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#informal" title="Appendix:Glossary">informal</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/bras_d%27honneur" title="bras d'honneur">bras d'honneur</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">obscene gesture</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="pt"><a href="/wiki/manguito#Portuguese" title="manguito">manguito</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Portugal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_13">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="pt">banana</strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span>, <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-pt p-form-of" lang="pt"><a href="/wiki/bananas#Portuguese" title="bananas">bananas</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/derogatory" title="derogatory">derogatory</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/wimp" title="wimp">wimp</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a weak or inconfident person</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="pt">Aquele rapaz é um <b>banana</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That guy is a <b>wimp</b>!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sardinian">Sardinian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Sardinian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href="/wiki/banana#Spanish" title="banana">banana</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wolof_language" class="extiw" title="w:Wolof language">Wolof</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="wo"><a href="/wiki/banaana#Wolof" title="banaana">banaana</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_10">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=72" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="sc">banana</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="sc"><a href="/wiki/bananas#Sardinian" title="bananas">bananas</a></b>)

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=74" title="Edit section: Serbo-Croatian">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=75" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wolof_language" class="extiw" title="w:Wolof language">Wolof</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="wo"><a href="/wiki/banaana#Wolof" title="banaana">banaana</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_11">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=76" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:Serbo-Croatian_pronunciation" title="Appendix:Serbo-Croatian pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/banǎːna/</span></li>
<li>Hyphenation: <span class="Latn" lang="sh">ba‧na‧na</span></li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_17">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=83" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="es">banana</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-es p-form-of" lang="es"><a href="/wiki/bananas#Spanish" title="bananas">bananas</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Argentina" class="extiw" title="w:Argentina">Argentina</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Colombia" class="extiw" title="w:Colombia">Colombia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ecuador" class="extiw" title="w:Ecuador">Ecuador</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Paraguay" class="extiw" title="w:Paraguay">Paraguay</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Uruguay" class="extiw" title="w:Uruguay">Uruguay</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="#English">banana</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">fruit</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="es"><a href="/wiki/pl%C3%A1tano#Spanish" title="plátano">plátano</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="es"><a href="/wiki/guineo#Spanish" title="guineo">guineo</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="es"><a href="/wiki/cambur#Spanish" title="cambur">cambur</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="es"><a href="/wiki/banano#Spanish" title="banano">banano</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=84" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li><i>banana</i> may also be used in Spain, to differentiate from <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href="/wiki/pl%C3%A1tano#Spanish" title="plátano">plátano</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">plantain</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; otherwise, <i>plátano</i> refers to either.</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_18">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=89" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><a href="#English">banana</a>
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1995</b>,  John Verhaar,  <cite>Toward a reference grammar of Tok Pisin: an experiment in corpus linguistics</cite>‎<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=4DeKkIzS8B4C&amp;pg=PA433#v=onepage&amp;q&amp;f=false">[1]</a></sup> (in English), <small><a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/0-8248-1672-2" title="Special:BookSources/0-8248-1672-2">→ISBN</a></small>, page 433:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="tpi">Mekim olsem pinis, orait tupela i planim taro na <b>banana</b>, na kumu, painap, kon, tomato, na kaukau tu.</span><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_11">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=banana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=91" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/banana#English" title="banana">banana</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wolof_language" class="extiw" title="w:Wolof language">Wolof</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="wo"><a href="/wiki/banaana#Wolof" title="banaana">banaana</a></i>, via Portuguese and/or Spanish.
</p>
